{"answers": ["nearby objects", "nearby"], "model_answer": "According to the provided documents, parallax is more pronounced with nearby stars. The documents state that the parallax of a star is defined as half of the angular distance that a star appears to move relative to the celestial sphere as Earth orbits the Sun. The smaller the distance to the star, the larger the parallax angle, making it easier to measure. Newton was the first to apply calculus to general physics, while Leibniz developed much of the notation used in calculus today.
